<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 1.01. Entry into a Material Definitive
Agreement.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Purchase and Sale Agreement</font></i>.
On December&nbsp;15, 2005, Kraft Foods Global,&nbsp;Inc. (&#147;Kraft&#148;), a wholly
owned indirect subsidiary of Kraft Foods Inc., entered into a Purchase and Sale
Agreement (the &#147;Purchase Agreement&#148;) with Altria Corporate Services,&nbsp;Inc.
(&#147;ALCS&#148;), pursuant to which ALCS assigned to Kraft, and Kraft assumed from
ALCS, ALCS&#146;s rights and obligations under a ground lease (the &#147;Ground Lease&#148;)
relating to an aircraft hangar located in Milwaukee, Wisconsin (the &#147;Real
Property&#148;). In addition, pursuant to the Purchase Agreement, ALCS sold to
Kraft, and Kraft purchased from ALCS, certain improvements and personal
property located on or related to the Real Property (collectively with the
rights and obligations under the Ground Lease, the &#147;Property&#148;). Under the terms
of the Purchase Agreement, Kraft paid to ALCS approximately $3.3 million in
consideration for acquiring the Property.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Amended and Restated Aircraft Management
Agreement</font></i>. In connection with the Purchase Agreement,
on December&nbsp;16, 2005 (the &#147;Closing Date&#148;), Kraft and ALCS entered into an
Amended and Restated Aircraft Management Agreement (the &#147;Amended and Restated
Aircraft Management Agreement&#148;), providing for ALCS to perform aircraft
management, pilot services, maintenance and other aviation services for Kraft
and to procure, at Kraft&#146;s expense, certain insurance coverage with respect to
specified aircraft owned by Kraft. The Amended and Restated Aircraft Management
Agreement amended and restated that certain Aircraft Management Agreement
entered into by Kraft and ALCS on December&nbsp;29, 2004 and was entered into
primarily as a result of Kraft&#146; s acquisition of the Property.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Environmental Agreement</font></i>.
In connection with the Purchase Agreement, on the Closing Date, Kraft and ALCS
entered into an Environmental Agreement (the &#147;Environmental Agreement&#148;),
pursuant to which ALCS agreed to remain responsible for, and to indemnify and
hold Kraft harmless from, all conditions, releases or discharges involving
hazardous or toxic substances on the Real Property occurring from September 1,
1993 to the Closing Date, and Kraft agreed to be responsible for, and to
indemnify and hold ALCS harmless from, all conditions, releases or discharges
involving hazardous or toxic substances on the Real Property occurring on or
after the Closing Date.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The foregoing descriptions of the Purchase
Agreement, Amended and Restated Aircraft Management Agreement and Environmental
Agreement are qualified in their entirety by reference to the complete terms
and conditions of the Purchase Agreement, Amended and Restated Aircraft
Management Agreement and Environmental Agreement, as the case may be, which are
attached as Exhibits 10.1, 10.2 and 10.3, respectively, to this Current Report
on Form&nbsp;8-K.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 9.01. Financial Statements and Exhibits.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

Report on Form&nbsp;8-K:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.78%;">

<body lang="EN-US">

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit&nbsp;10.1</font></b></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">PURCHASE
AND SALE AGREEMENT</font></u></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This Purchase and Sale Agreement is made as of this 15th day of
December, 2005 (this &#147;Agreement&#148;), by and between <b><font style="font-weight:bold;">ALTRIA CORPORATE SERVICES, INC. (f/k/a PHILIP MORRIS MANAGEMENT
CORPORATION)</font></b>, a New York corporation (&#147;Seller&#148;) and <b><font style="font-weight:bold;">KRAFT FOODS GLOBAL, INC.</font></b> (&#147;Buyer&#148;), a
Delaware corporation.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">W I T N E S S E T H</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">WHEREAS, Seller and Milwaukee County, Wisconsin are parties to certain
Lease Agreement, dated July&nbsp;14, 1980, Airport Agreement No.&nbsp;HP-695,
as amended by Amendment No.&nbsp;1 to Airport Lease Agreement No.&nbsp;HP-695
as of December&nbsp;31, 1995 and Amendment No.&nbsp;2 to Airport Lease
Agreement No.&nbsp;HP-695 as of December&nbsp;16, 2005 (the &#147;Lease&#148;) with
respect to certain property located at General Mitchell International Airport (&#147;Airport&#148;);
and</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">WHEREAS, Seller desires to sell and transfer to Buyer, and Buyer
desires to purchase and accept from Seller, all of Seller&#146;s rights, title and
interests in the Lease and certain other property described herein on the terms
and conditions hereinafter set forth,</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the foregoing premises and of the
mutual covenants, representations and warranties herein set forth, the parties
hereto hereby covenant and agree as follows:</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Purchase
and Sale</u>.&#160; Seller hereby agrees to
sell, assign, convey, transfer and deliver and Buyer hereby agrees to purchase,
accept and receive the following property (collectively, the &#147;Property&#148;):</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>All
of Seller&#146;s right, title and interest as lessee under the Lease for property
located at 530 East College Avenue, Milwaukee, Wisconsin, and described on <u>Exhibit&nbsp;A</u>
(the &#147;Real Property&#148;);</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>All
fixtures or real property improvements owned by Seller and located on the Real
Property, as described on <u>Exhibit&nbsp;A </u>(the &#147;Improvements&#148;);</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
personal property listed on <u>Exhibit&nbsp;B</u> (&#147;Personal Property&#148;); and</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Such
other personal property located on the Real Property on the date of Closing (&#147;Other
Personal Property&#148;), but excluding aircraft spare parts, telecommunications
equipment, and information technology systems.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Purchase
Price and Other Payments</u>.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
total purchase price for the Property shall be Three Million Two Hundred
Ninety-Eight Thousand Two Hundred Thirty-Seven Dollars ($3,298,237) (the &#147;Purchase
Price&#148;) and shall be allocated as follows:</p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
purchase price for the Real Property, Improvements and the Other Personal
Property shall be Three Million Dollars ($3,000,000), payable by wire transfer,
at the consummation of the transactions contemplated in Section&nbsp;1 hereof
(the &#147;Closing&#148;).</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
purchase price for the Personal Property shall be Two Hundred Ninety-Eight
Thousand Two Hundred Thirty-Seven Dollars ($298,237), payable by wire transfer,
at the consummation of transactions contemplated in Section&nbsp;1 hereof.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Other
payments shall be made to Buyer or Seller, as the case may be as follows:</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Net
real estate taxes (if any), under the Lease shall be prorated as of the date of
closing, with all such items through the date of closing accruing to
Seller.&#160; Taxes shall be prorated based on
the most current available bill.&#160; Special
assessments, if any, for work actually commenced or levied prior to the date of
Closing shall be paid by Seller.&#160; All
other special assessments or other charges shall be paid by Buyer.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>On
the Closing Date, Seller shall receive a payment from the Buyer for the average
blended cost of all fuel located on the Real Property.&#160; The determination of the exact amount shall
be made on the Closing Date and the payment shall be made at Closing.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Buyer&#146;s
Conditions Precedent</u>.&#160; Buyer&#146;s
obligation to pay the purchase price set forth in Section&nbsp;1 and to
conclude the purchase transaction as set forth herein is subject to the
fulfillment, of each of the following conditions:</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>One
or more inspections of the Property to be conducted by December&nbsp;10, 2005,
including without limitation the auditing, sampling and testing for the
presence of any hazardous or solid waste or any other condition adversely affecting
the environment (including air, water, or soil), conducted by or on behalf of
Buyer, at Buyer&#146;s expense, at reasonable times upon reasonable notice to Seller
and for the purpose of Buyer determining, in its sole judgment, whether the
Property, including without limitation its fire protection and other systems,
has any defects or conditions of any nature that, if not corrected, repaired,
replaced or repaired, would shorten or adversely affect the value, utility, or
useful life of the Property to Buyer (&#147;Defect&#148;).&#160; Buyer shall not cause any unreasonable
interference with the conduct of Seller&#146;s business on the Property, and Buyer
shall repair all damage to the Property caused by Buyer, or its contractors or
agents.&#160; Buyer shall indemnify and hold
Seller harmless from any claim, loss, cost, damage or expense arising from
damage to the Property or from personal injuries to or death of any third
person.&#160; Seller, or its agent, may
accompany Buyer or Buyer&#146;s agent during such inspections.&#160; This condition precedent for inspections
shall be considered waived unless Buyer, by December&nbsp;10, 2005,&#160; notifies Seller, in writing, of those
Defects.&#160; Seller may notify Buyer in
writing within five (5)&nbsp;business days of receipt of Buyer&#146;s notice of
Defect of its election to cure such identified Defects prior to Closing, in
which case this Agreement shall continue and Seller shall promptly undertake
efforts for such cure.&#160; If Seller fails
to provide such notice within the time stated or if Buyer notifies Seller in
writing within five (5)&nbsp;business days of Seller&#146;s notice that Seller&#146;s
efforts to cure or the time needed for Seller to cure are unsatisfactory in
Buyer&#146;s sole judgment, then Buyer may terminate its obligation to close
hereunder.</p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Seller&#146;s
delivery to Buyer, at or prior to Closing, written confirmation that the
Milwaukee, Wisconsin County Board approved the Assignment of Lease Airport
Agreement No.&nbsp;HP-695 (&#147;Assignment&#148;) from Seller to Buyer with
modifications described in the Amendment No.&nbsp;3 to Airport Lease Agreement No.&nbsp;HR-695
(&#147;Amendment&#148;) attached as Exhibit&nbsp;C-1.&#160;
Said approval shall be deemed satisfied if an assignment substantially
in the form of Exhibit&nbsp;C-2 is delivered, the Milwaukee County Board
approves a resolution authorizing amendments to the Lease as required by this
subparagraph, and the Milwaukee County Director of Public Works (or his
designee) executes such Assignment and Amendment.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
representations and warranties made by Seller contained or referenced in this
Agreement shall be true and correct in all material respects on the date hereof
and on and as of the Closing as though made at that time.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Title
Evidence</u>.&#160; At least five (5)&nbsp;business
days prior to Closing, Seller shall provide Buyer with a commitment from Ticor
Title Insurance Company (the &#147;Title Company&#148;) to issue a leasehold policy of
title insurance (with extended coverage, if available) on Buyer&#146;s interest in
the Lease, in the amount of the purchase price for the Real Property and
Improvements showing lessee&#146;s interest in the Lease in Buyer, as of a date no
more than ten (10)&nbsp;days before such title commitment is provided Buyer, to
be in the condition called for in this Agreement and further subject only to
such liens as will be paid out of the proceeds at Closing.&#160; Buyer shall notify Seller of any valid
objections to title in writing at least three (3)&nbsp;business days prior to
Closing.&#160; Seller shall have a reasonable
time, not to exceed thirty (30) days, to remove the objections and Closing
shall be extended as necessary for this purpose.&#160; If Seller is unwilling or unable to remove
such objections, Buyer shall thereupon have the option to terminate this
Agreement or waive such objections and proceed to close this transaction.&#160; Buyer recognizes that the Real Property and
Improvements are part of the Milwaukee County Airport.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Conveyance</u>.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Upon
Buyer&#146;s payment of the Purchase Price, Seller shall convey the Property to
Buyer at Closing by assignment of lease, bill of sale and a special warranty
deed, as appropriate, free and clear of all mortgages, liens, pledges, security
interests and encumbrances, except municipal and zoning ordinances, recorded
easements for public utilities serving the Real Property, recorded building and
use restrictions and covenants, any deed restriction affecting the Real
Property required by the Wisconsin Department of Natural Resources, taxes
levied in the year of Closing, matters listed (in accordance with Section&nbsp;4
above) on the Preliminary Title Commitment of Ticor Title Insurance Company
dated March&nbsp;31, 2005, attached as Exhibit&nbsp;D, and any encumbrances
accepted by Buyer pursuant to Section&nbsp;4 hereof, provided none of the
foregoing prohibit the current use of the Property (&#147;Permitted Encumbrances&#148;).&#160; Seller shall further complete and execute all
documents necessary to record this conveyance.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>At
Closing, Seller shall execute and deliver to Buyer, or cause to be executed and
delivered to Buyer, all of the following (collectively, &#147;Seller&#146;s Closing Documents&#148;):</p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Deed</font></b>.&#160; Special Warranty Deed conveying to Buyer all
of the Real Property and Improvements, free and clear of all encumbrances
claimed by, through or under Seller, except only the Permitted Encumbrances.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">FIRPTA Affidavit</font></b>.&#160; An affidavit of
non-foreign status properly containing such information as is required by IRC Section&nbsp;1445(b)(2)&nbsp;and
its regulations.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Title-related Documents</font></b>.&#160;
Such affidavits of Seller or other documents as may be reasonably
required by the Title Company to record the deed and issue the Title Policy
required by this Agreement.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(4)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Certificate</font></b>.&#160; A certificate signed by
an authorized agent of Seller and dated as of the Closing Date reaffirming the
truth, correctness, and completeness of all of Seller&#146;s representations and
warranties under this Agreement.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(5)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Files and Records</font></b>.&#160; Copies of files related
to the Property in Seller&#146;s possession and located at the Real Property on the
Closing Date.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(6)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Resolutions</font></b>.&#160; Corporate resolutions (or a secretary&#146;s
certificate) of Seller in such form as may be reasonably satisfactory to the
Title Company to evidence Seller&#146;s authority to transfer the Property.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(7)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Bill of Sale</font></b>.&#160; A bill of sale conveying all Personal
Property, Improvements and Other Personal Property free and clear of all claims
under or through the Seller.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(8)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Lease Amendment</font></b>.&#160; Lease Amendment in the form required by Section&nbsp;3(b)&nbsp;of
this Agreement, together with an executed copy of the Lease.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(9)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Title Insurance</font></b>.&#160; Title Policy required by this Agreement,
together with the following endorsements (or the substantial, local equivalent
of such endorsements) relating to the Real Property, to the extent that such
endorsements are customarily available in Wisconsin (altogether, the &#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Endorsements</font></b>&#148;):&#160; a &#147;gap&#148; endorsement; an access endorsement;
and an ALTA 9 (owner&#146;s) restrictions, encroachments, and minerals endorsement.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Buyer&#146;s
Closing Deliveries.&#160; At Closing, Buyer
will execute and deliver to Seller, or cause to be executed and delivered to
Seller, all of the following (collectively, &#147;Buyer&#146;s Closing Documents&#148;):</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Purchase Price</font></b>.<b><font style="font-weight:bold;"> </font></b>&#160;The Purchase Price, plus or minus prorations
and other adjustments described in Sections 2(b)(i)&nbsp;and 2(b)(ii), if any,
by wire transfer of immediately available funds.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Title Documents</font></b>.<b><font style="font-weight:bold;"> </font></b>&#160;Such affidavits of Buyer or other documents as
may be reasonably required by the Title Company in order to record the deed and
issue the Title Policy (with endorsements) required by this Agreement.</p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Certificate</font></b>.&#160; A certificate signed by
an authorized agent of Buyer and dated as of the Closing Date reaffirming the
truth, correctness, and completeness of all Buyer&#146;s representations and
warranties under this Agreement.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(4)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Resolutions</font></b>.&#160; Corporate resolutions or a secretary&#146;s
certificate of Buyer in such form as may be reasonably satisfactory to the
Title Company to evidence Buyer&#146;s authority to carry out the transfer that is
the subject of this Agreement.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Joint Closing Deliveries.</font></b>&#160; At Closing, Seller and Buyer shall jointly
execute and deliver the following:</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Closing Statement</font></b>.&#160; A closing and proration
statement, prepared by Seller and reasonably acceptable to Buyer.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Real Estate Transfer Returns</font></b>.&#160; Properly completed copies of any real estate
transfer return, gains tax form, or other documentation required in Wisconsin
to transfer the Real Property or record any deed.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Lease Assignment</font></b>.&#160; Lease Assignment for the Real Property and
Improvements in the form set forth in this Agreement</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(4)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Miscellaneous</font></b>.<b><font style="font-weight:bold;"> </font></b>&#160;Such other documents, instruments, and
affidavits as shall be reasonably necessary to consummate the transaction
contemplated by this Agreement (including, without limitation, a written assignment
conveying to Buyer all of Seller&#146;s right, title, and interest in and to any
contract or license concerning the Property that may freely be transferred
without the consent or approval of any third party).</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:2.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Closing</u>.&#160; This transaction is to be closed at
Milwaukee, Wisconsin, on or before December&nbsp;16, 2005 (&#147;Closing Date&#148;), or
at such other time or location as the parties may agree in writing.&#160; Occupancy and use of the Real Property shall
be given to Buyer at Closing or at such other time and subject to such terms
and conditions as the parties may agree in writing.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Closing Costs
Shall Be Allocated As Follows:</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Title Insurance</font></b>.<b><font style="font-weight:bold;"> </font></b>&#160;Seller shall pay the cost of the Title Policy
required under this Agreement.&#160; Buyer
shall pay the cost of the endorsements to the Title Policy.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Closing Fee</font></b>.<b><font style="font-weight:bold;"> </font></b>&#160;Seller and Buyer will each pay one-half of any
reasonable and customary closing fee charged by the Title Company (including,
without limitation, any reasonable and customary fee for an escrow).</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Transfer Tax</font></b>.<b><font style="font-weight:bold;"> </font></b>&#160;With respect to any real estate transfer fee,
transfer tax, or other fee charged by any pertinent governmental authority as
an incident to transfer of title in the Real Property (in each instance, a &#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Transfer Tax</font></b>&#148;), the parties agree that Seller shall pay any
Transfer Tax owing with respect to transfer of title in any Real Property.&#160; Buyer shall pay any sales or use taxes
applicable to the Personal Property and Other Personal Property.</p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Recording Costs</font></b>.&#160; Seller shall pay the

Agreement.&#160; Buyer shall pay recording
fees owing to record the deed.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(e)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Attorney&#146;s Fees</font></b>.<b><font style="font-weight:bold;"> </font></b>&#160;Each Party shall pay its own attorneys fees.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(f)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Other Costs</font></b>.<b><font style="font-weight:bold;"> </font></b>&#160;All other costs shall be allocated in
accordance with the customs prevailing in similar transactions in Wisconsin.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Representations
and Warranties.</u></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Seller
hereby represents and warrants as of the date hereof:</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Seller
has the corporate power and authority to execute and deliver this Agreement and
as of Closing will have the corporate power and authority to perform its
obligations hereunder and to consummate the transactions contemplated hereby;</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>This
Agreement constitutes a valid and legally binding obligation enforceable
against the Seller in accordance with the terms hereof, except as may be
limited by applicable bankruptcy, reorganization, insolvency, moratorium or
other similar laws from time to time in effect affecting creditors&#146; rights
generally, or equitable principles of general application;</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Seller
is not obligated in any manner to pay any finder&#146;s fee or brokerage or similar
commission in respect to the transactions contemplated by this Agreement and
has taken no action that would obligate Buyer to pay any such fee or
commission;</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Seller
has no notice or knowledge of any:&#160; (1)&nbsp;planned
or commenced public improvements which may result in special assessments; (2)&nbsp;planned
public improvements which would materially affect the real estate except for
proposals or master plans of Milwaukee County, Wisconsin; or (3)&nbsp;official
written order requiring repair, alteration or correction of any existing
condition on the Real Property or Improvements;</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(e)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>To
the best of Seller&#146;s knowledge, no consent, approval or authorization of, or
declaration or filing with, any governmental authority is required for valid
execution and delivery of this Agreement and the consummation of the
transactions contemplated hereby, except for the approval of the Milwaukee
County Board and the Wisconsin Department of Natural Resources as set forth
herein; and</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(f)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Other
than as specifically set forth in Section&nbsp;7.1 (d), the Property will be
sold &#147;AS IS&#148; with no warranties or representations by Seller, whether express
or implied.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

hereby represents and warrants as follows:</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Buyer

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>This
Agreement constitutes a valid and legally binding obligation enforceable
against the Buyer in accordance with the terms hereof, except as may be limited
by applicable bankruptcy, reorganization, insolvency, moratorium or other
similar laws from time to time in effect affecting creditors&#146; rights generally,
or equitable principles of general application;</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Buyer
is not obligated in any manner to pay any finder&#146;s fee or brokerage or similar
commission in respect to the transactions contemplated by this Agreement and
has taken no action that would obligate Seller to pay any such fee or
commission.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Damage</u>.&#160; Prior to the Closing, if any part of the
Property is damaged in an amount of not more than $50,000, Seller shall be
obligated to repair or replace the same to equal or better condition than prior
to the damage.&#160; If such damage shall
exceed $50,000, Seller shall within five (5)&nbsp;business days inform Buyer in
writing of the extent that insurance proceeds will be available with respect to
the damage.&#160; Within five (5)&nbsp;days
after receipt of such notice from Seller regarding the availability of
insurance proceeds, Buyer, at its sole option, may cancel this Agreement by
written notice to Seller.&#160; If Buyer
elects not to terminate this Agreement, Seller shall not be required to repair
the Property, but Buyer shall be entitled to receive all insurance proceeds
relating to the damage.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Default.</u></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>If
Buyer defaults in its obligation to consummate this Agreement, Seller shall be
entitled, at Seller&#146;s sole election, (i)&nbsp;to terminate this Agreement and
assert a claim for Seller&#146;s costs, expenses, and other damages in connection
with this Agreement, which claim shall not exceed the sum of Three Hundred
Thousand and No/100 ($300,000) United States Dollars (USD Three Hundred
Thousand),&#160; (ii)&nbsp;close the
transaction contemplated by this Agreement without waiving any claim of
default, and thereafter assert a claim for Seller&#146;s costs, expenses, and other
damages in connection with Buyer&#146;s default under this Agreement, which claim
shall not exceed the sum of Three Hundred Thousand and No/100 United States
Dollars (USD $300,000), or (iii)&nbsp;pursue any other remedy available to
Seller at law or in equity (including, without limitation, an action for Seller&#146;s
damages and an action for specific performance), either as an alternative to
the remedies set forth in this Section&nbsp;9(a)&nbsp;or in conjunction
therewith.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>If
Seller defaults in its obligation to consummate this Agreement, Buyer shall be
entitled, as its sole remedy,&#160; to assert
a claim for Buyer&#146;s costs, expenses, and other damages in connection with this
Agreement, which claim shall not exceed the sum of Three Hundred Thousand and
No/100 United States Dollars (USD $300,000).</p>

  <td width="50%" colspan="4" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:50.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
