<body lang="EN-US">

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit&nbsp;10.2</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">AMENDED AND RESTATED<br>
<u>AIRCRAFT MANAGEMENT AGREEMENT</u></font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">THIS AMENDED AND RESTATED AIRCRAFT MANAGEMENT
AGREEMENT</font></b> (the &#147;Agreement&#148;) is made and entered into
as of this 16th day of December, 2005 (the &#147;Effective Date&#148;), by and between
KRAFT FOODS GLOBAL, INC., a Delaware corporation with a principal place of
business located at Three Lakes Drive, Northfield, IL 60093 (&#147;Kraft&#148;), and
ALTRIA CORPORATE SERVICES, INC., a New York corporation with a principal place
of business located at 120 Park Avenue, New York, NY 10017 (&#147;Manager&#148;).</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">WITNESSETH:</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">WHEREAS</font></b>, Kraft
rightfully possesses the aircraft described in Exhibit&nbsp;A (which may be
amended from time to time by mutual agreement of the parties to provide for
substitution, replacement, addition or removal of certain aircraft)
(collectively, the &#147;Aircraft&#148;);</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">WHEREAS</font></b>, Kraft
desires Manager to continue to provide aircraft management, pilot services,
maintenance and other aviation services (the &#147;Services&#148;) to Kraft to allow
Kraft to continue to conduct operations pursuant to Federal Aviation
Regulations (&#147;FARs&#148;) Part&nbsp;91 under Kraft&#146;s operational control pursuant to
the terms and conditions of this Agreement;</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">WHEREAS</font></b>, Manager has
flight department personnel experienced in the business of managing, operating,
maintaining, and scheduling corporate aircraft and desires to continue to
perform these services for Kraft on the terms and conditions stated herein;</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">WHEREAS</font></b>, Kraft and
Manager are parties to an Aircraft Management Agreement dated as of December&nbsp;29,
2004 (the &#147;2004 Management Agreement&#148;);</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">WHEREAS</font></b>, on December&nbsp;16,
2005, Kraft acquired title to the Hangar Facility situated at the Base of
Operations and entered into an assignment of the Ground Lease pursuant to which
Kraft became the lessee of the Airport Leased Premises (the terms Hangar
Facility, Base of Operations, Ground Lease and Airport Leased Premises are
defined in Article&nbsp;11.1 hereof); and</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">WHEREAS</font></b>, Kraft and
Manager desire to amend and restate the 2004 Management Agreement primarily as
the result of Kraft&#146;s acquiring title to the Hangar Facility and becoming the
lessee under the Ground Lease.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">NOW THEREFORE</font></b>, in
consideration of the promises and the mutual covenants contained herein, and
for good and valuable consideration, Kraft and Manager hereby agree as follows:</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\mgovind\05-21974-1\task711885\21974-1-kc.htm',USER='mgovindarajulu',CD='Dec 18 11:25 2005' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h1 style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">ARTICLE&nbsp;ONE</font></b><font style="text-transform:none;"><br>
TERM</font></h1>

<h1 style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;">&nbsp;</font></h1>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Term</u>.
The term of this Agreement (the &#147;Term&#148;) shall commence on the Effective Date
and shall remain in effect until such time as it has been terminated as to the
Services in accordance with Article&nbsp;1.2 below.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.2</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Termination</u>.
Either Party may terminate this Agreement without cause by providing one
hundred twenty (120) days&#146; prior written notice to the other Party or as
otherwise agreed between the Parties hereto.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.3</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Accounting
after Termination</u>. Within one hundred twenty (120) days after the
termination date, Manager shall make a full accounting and the parties shall
settle all accounts between them.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.4</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Redelivery
of Aircraft and Records</u>. Upon termination of this Agreement, Manager shall
redeliver the Aircraft, along with all Aircraft-specific books and records to
Kraft.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.5</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Termination
Assistance Services</u>.&#160; Manager agrees
that, upon termination of this Agreement, and at Kraft&#146;s expense, Manager will
cooperate in good faith with Kraft to provide Kraft (or its designee) with
reasonable assistance to make an orderly transition from Manager to another
supplier of the Services. Transition assistance services shall include the
following:</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Developing
a transition plan with assistance from Kraft or its designee;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Providing
training to Kraft personnel or its designee&#146;s personnel to perform Services;
and</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Organizing
and delivering to Kraft records and documents necessary to allow continuation
of the Services, including delivering such materials in electronic forms and
versions as requested by Kraft.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h1 style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">ARTICLE&nbsp;TWO</font></b><font style="text-transform:none;"><br>
MANAGER&#146;S OBLIGATIONS</font></h1>

<h1 style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;">&nbsp;</font></h1>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Provision
of Aircraft Management and Aviation Services</u>. Manager hereby agrees to
manage the Aircraft and furnish certain aviation support services described
below to Kraft during the Term.&#160; Such
services shall be provided in accordance with any applicable FARs and in
accordance with Manager&#146;s established procedures with respect to its own
aircraft, as such procedures may be modified from time to time, including but
not limited to the Altria Corporate Services,&nbsp;Inc. Aviation and Travel
Services Policy and Operations Manual (the &#147;Manual&#148;).</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.2</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Pilot
and Flight Attendant Services</u>. Manager agrees to provide pilot services to
Kraft. Manager agrees to employ and provide a sufficient number of fully
qualified pilots to operate the Aircraft in accordance with the Manual.&#160; Manager reserves the right to utilize the
services of temporary qualified pilots, acceptable to both Manager and Kraft,
to supplement full-time staff, from time to time, when deemed necessary by
Manager.&#160; It is agreed that the term &#147;qualified
pilot&#148; shall be deemed to refer to an individual who meets the following
minimum requirements:</h2>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Holds
a valid Airline Transport Pilot&#146;s Certificate with appropriate category, class
and type ratings for the Aircraft;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Holds
a current first class medical certificate in accordance with FAR &#167;61.23(a)(1);</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Is
current with respect to FAR Part&nbsp;61, to conduct operations under FAR Part&nbsp;91;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Is
familiar with Manager&#146;s written policies and procedures;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(e)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Has
satisfactorily completed a recommended or approved ground and flight training
course for the Aircraft;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(f)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Is
approved as pilot with respect to the Aircraft insurance coverage; and</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(g)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Is
approved as a pilot under the Manual.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Manager agrees to provide flight attendant
services to Kraft.&#160; Manager agrees to
employ and provide a sufficient number of fully qualified flight attendants to
perform flight attendant services in accordance with the Manual.&#160; Manager reserves the right to utilize the
services of temporary qualified flight attendants, acceptable to both Manager
and Kraft, to supplement full-time staff, from time to time, when deemed necessary
by Manager.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In accordance with the applicable FARs, each
flight crew member provided by Manager will exercise all of his or her duties
and responsibilities with the highest regard for the safety of each flight
conducted hereunder.&#160; Kraft specifically
agrees that the pilot-in-command, in his or her sole discretion, may terminate
any flight, refuse to commence any flight, or take any other such action which
in the considered judgment of such pilot in command is necessitated by safety
considerations. No such action by the pilot in command shall create or support
any liability for loss, injury, damage or delay to Kraft or any other
person.&#160; Kraft further agrees that
Manager shall not be liable for delay or failure to furnish or return the
Aircraft or flight crew pursuant to this Agreement when such failure is caused
by government regulation or authority, mechanical difficulty, war, civil
commotion, strikes or labor disputes, weather conditions or acts of God or is
necessary to adhere to the requirements of the Manual.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.3</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Maintenance
and Inspections of Aircraft.</u> Manager shall be responsible for providing
maintenance, preventive maintenance, and required or otherwise necessary
inspections of the Aircraft. No period of maintenance, preventive maintenance
or inspection shall be delayed or postponed for the purpose of scheduling the
Aircraft, unless said maintenance or inspection can be safely conducted at a
later time in compliance with all applicable laws and regulations, and within
the sound discretion of the assigned pilot in command and Manager&#146;s maintenance
manager.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">It is expected by the parties that Manager
will perform, or arrange to be performed by qualified third parties, all
required pre-flight inspections and maintenance of the Aircraft, will keep the
interior and the exterior of the Aircraft clean, and will repair discrepancies
and perform scheduled inspections.&#160;
Subject to the provisions of Article&nbsp;3.4 below, it is expected by
the parties that Manager or Kraft may subcontract with outside maintenance
providers to perform any additional necessary maintenance on the Aircraft.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kraft appoints Manager as its agent for the
limited purpose of executing, for and on behalf of Kraft, any maintenance
program and maintenance inspection agreements or any other </font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">agreement as
shall be necessary in order for Manager to fulfill its obligations under this
Agreement.&#160; Kraft agrees to indemnify and
hold Manager harmless from and against any claims, damages, losses or expenses
arising pursuant to any such maintenance program and maintenance inspection
agreements, or any other agreement necessary in order for Manager to fulfill
its obligations under this Agreement.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.4</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Logbooks
and Records</u>. Manager shall maintain all logbooks and records pertaining to
the Aircraft in accordance with applicable FARs.&#160; Manager shall make such logbooks and records
available for examination and copying by Kraft or Kraft&#146;s duly authorized
agents, at Kraft&#146;s reasonable advance request, at the location of such books
and records at the Hangar Facility.&#160; At
the termination of this Agreement, Manager shall deliver such logbooks and
records to Kraft.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.5</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Additional
Duties of Manager</u>. In addition to those duties assumed by Manager elsewhere
herein, Manager also agrees to perform the following:</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Arrange
for and coordinate and schedule&nbsp;use of the Aircraft;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Arrange
for aircraft commissary, catering and rental car, limousine or taxi cab
passenger ground transportation, as requested by Kraft;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Utilize
and maintain the Hangar Facility and perform Kraft&#146;s maintenance obligations
under Sections 9 and 10 of the Ground Lease in order to provide Services
pursuant to this Agreement, including but not limited to:&#160; assisting the flight crew in the performance
of their duties; achieving scheduling of flights and flight personnel, flight
following and communication; performing routine scheduled and unscheduled
maintenance to the Aircraft; and assisting Kraft in the planning and support of
Kraft&#146;s flight operation;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Advise,
assist and cooperate with Kraft in establishing the annual budget (&#147;Original
Budget&#148; or &#147;OB&#148;) and semi-annual budget update (&#147;Second Revised Forecast&#148; or &#147;SRF&#148;)
for each year during the Term for fixed and variable expenses respecting the
Aircraft, the Hangar Facility and the Airport Leased Premises (including the
performance of Manager&#146;s responsibilities hereunder).&#160; Manager shall also assist Kraft in the
process of transitioning to Kraft the direct payment by Kraft of all such fixed
and variable expenses (except for employee costs and insurance expenses which
shall continue to be paid by Manager and subsequently billed to Kraft, as
provided in Articles 3 and 5 of this Agreement);</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(e)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>At
Kraft&#146;s request, arrange for backup aircraft coverage with a commercial
certificated air carrier or other provider operating in accordance with FARs
and acceptable to Manager and Kraft when the Aircraft is unavailable for Kraft&#146;s
use due to scheduled or unscheduled maintenance.&#160; Manager shall provide Kraft with a copy of
its list of acceptable providers upon request;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(f)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Assist
Kraft in obtaining and maintaining such insurance covering the Aircraft and its
operation as further described in Article&nbsp;5.1 below;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(g)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Provide
such proof of insurance as required of Manager pursuant to Article&nbsp;5.1(g)&nbsp;below;
and</h3>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(h)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Arrange
for initial and recurrent training for each flight crew member, maintenance
technician and dispatcher.</h3>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h1 style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">ARTICLE&nbsp;THREE</font></b><font style="text-transform:none;"><br>
KRAFT&#146;S OBLIGATIONS</font></h1>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Operational
Control and Possession, Command and Control</u>.&#160; It is hereby agreed and acknowledged between
Kraft and Manager that during all phases of flights conducted under this
Agreement, Kraft shall retain and have (i)&nbsp;operational control of the
Aircraft, and (ii)&nbsp;possession, command and control of the Aircraft.&#160; In addition, Kraft further acknowledges
operational control by exercising Kraft&#146;s authority over initiating, conducting
and terminating each flight.&#160; Kraft
chooses not to hire its own pilots but contract for the pilot services of
Manager. Although the flight crew is supplied by Manager for Kraft&#146;s flights,
the flight crew is under the exclusive command and control of Kraft in all
phases of those flights and at all times. Kraft acknowledges that all of Kraft&#146;s
flights are classified as &#147;noncommercial&#148; for Federal Aviation regulatory
purposes and, for Federal excise tax purposes, are subject to the appropriate
federal tax on aviation fuels. In exercising operational control, Kraft shall
comply with the FARs, insurance requirements and any pertinent regulations of
the United States or any country where the Aircraft may be operated from time
to time.&#160; Kraft shall operate the
Aircraft in accordance with FAR Part&nbsp;91.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.2</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Advance
Notification</u>. Kraft shall provide Manager with information regarding proposed
flight schedules as far in advance of any given flight as possible.&#160; Information that must be provided to Manager
shall be in a format mutually acceptable to the parties and shall include the
following information for each proposed flight:</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Name
of requisitioner;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Date
requisition prepared;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Proposed
departure airport;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Proposed
destination airport;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(e)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Date
and time of flight;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(f)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
number, names and social security numbers of anticipated employee passengers
and the flight legs on which each will travel;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(g)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
number, names, addresses, telephone numbers and social security numbers of
anticipated non-employee passengers and the flight legs on which each will
travel;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(h)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
nature and extent of any non-customary luggage and/or cargo, to include
firearms and/or hazardous materials, to be carried;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
date and time of a return flight, if any;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(j)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Ground
transportation requests;</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(k)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Special
catering requests; and</h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(l)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Any
other information concerning the proposed flight that may be pertinent or
required by the other party.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kraft shall ensure that all passengers meet
all applicable requirements of US and foreign customs during travel aboard the
Aircraft.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Manager hereby designates Drew Barnes,
telephone (414) 574-2101, as its contact for aircraft scheduling. Manager may
change its contact for aircraft scheduling by providing written notice of such
change to Kraft in accordance with Article&nbsp;11.3 below.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kraft is currently not a &#147;citizen of the
United States&#148; as defined in 49 U.S.C. &#167;40102(a)(15), and is, therefore,
required to comply with the Department of Transportation regulations set forth
in 14 C.F.R. Part&nbsp;375, one effect of which is to prohibit carriage of
candidates in elections where payment for the carriage is required.&#160; During any time when Kraft is a &#147;citizen of
the United States&#148; as defined in 49 U.S.C. &#167;40102(a)(15), with respect to any
persons required by federal or state law to make payment for such flights,
Kraft agrees to comply with FAR 91.321 and to provide Manager with advance
notification and such additional information as may be reasonably requested by
Manager.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.3</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Management
Fee and Variable Expenses</u>.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Kraft
shall pay Manager a monthly management fee in order to reimburse Manager for a
ratable (i.e., 1/12<sup>th</sup>) portion of Manager&#146;s fixed annual (i)&nbsp;employee
costs for Manager&#146;s flight department senior management, to the extent such
senior management is engaged in providing services under this Agreement, and (ii)&nbsp;insurance
expenses associated with the performance of Manager&#146;s obligations and duties
under this Agreement.&#160; Kraft shall also
pay all other fixed expenses associated with its use of the Aircraft and
operation of the Aircraft and the utilization and maintenance of the Hangar
Facility and the Airport Leased Premises, whether incurred directly by Kraft or
incurred by Manager in the performance of its services under this Agreement and
billed back to Kraft, and shall pay to Manager the employee costs of Manager&#146;s
personnel based at the Hangar Facility who are engaged in the provision of
services under this Agreement.&#160; (All
fixed employee costs to be paid by Kraft hereunder shall include a 5% mark-up).</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Kraft
shall pay all variable expenses associated with its use of the Aircraft and
operation of the Aircraft under this Agreement and the utilization and
maintenance of the Hangar Facility and the Airport Leased Premises whether
incurred directly by Kraft or incurred by Manager in the performance of its
services under this Agreement and billed back to Kraft.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Manager
shall not, without the prior consent of Kraft, perform any capital improvement
on the Hangar Facility having an anticipated cost exceeding $10,000 unless such
capital improvement is provided for in the then-current OB or SRF.&#160; In the event that, in the reasonable judgment
of Manager, any repair or maintenance of the Hangar Facility (not provided for
in the the-current OB or SRF) is necessary or appropriate, Manager is
authorized to perform such Hangar Facility repair or maintenance at Kraft&#146;s
expense.&#160; Manager shall use all
reasonable efforts under the circumstances to notify Kraft in advance of any
Hangar Facility repair or maintenance expense not provided for in the
then-current OB or SRF which has an anticipated cost exceeding $10,000.&#160; Any consent or notification under this Article&nbsp;3.3(c)&nbsp;may
be given orally.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Manager
shall not, without the prior consent of Kraft, perform any capital improvement
on any of the Aircraft having an anticipated cost exceeding $100,000 unless
such capital improvement is provided for in the then-current OB or SRF.&#160; Any capital improvement </h3>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">performed by the Manager on any of the Aircraft shall be consistent
with the provisions of Article&nbsp;7 hereof.&#160;
Kraft shall also pay for all alterations, modifications, additions or

the time Manager performs such services.&#160;
In the event that, in the reasonable judgment of Manager, any repair or

or maintenance at Kraft&#146;s expense.&#160;

provided for in the then-current OB or SRF which has an anticipated cost
exceeding $100,000.&#160; Any consent or
notification under this Article&nbsp;3.3(d)may be given orally.</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(e)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Kraft

Lease.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.4</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Payment
of Fixed and Variable Expenses</u>.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Kraft
shall pay Manager through inter-company cash transfer the monthly management fee
on or before the third Wednesday of each month during the Term hereof.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Manager
shall deliver to Kraft, on or about the 15th day of each month, an invoice for
the aggregate fixed expenses (to the extent not included in the management fee)
and variable expenses incurred for the previous month and paid by Manager on
behalf of Kraft.&#160; Kraft will pay the
amount specified on such invoice to Manager, through inter-company cash
transfer no later than the third Wednesday of the month following the month that
such invoice was sent to Kraft.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>At
the end of each six months during the term of the Agreement, Manager will
review the fixed expenses comprising the management fee actually incurred by
Manager (collectively, &#147;Actual Cost&#148;) during the previous six months.&#160; In the event that Manager determines that the
Actual Cost differs from the aggregate fixed expenses comprising the management
fee as set forth in the preceding OB or SRF (as the case may be) by more than
2%, Manager will deliver to Kraft documentation for such Actual Cost and the
Parties will adjust the monthly management fee accordingly, retroactively or
prospectively.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On or before November&nbsp;15 of each
calendar year, in connection with the annual review of services provided to
Kraft Foods Inc. and its wholly owned subsidiaries under the Services Agreement
dated as of January&nbsp;1, 2001, an estimate of the fixed and variable
expenses for the next calendar year will be submitted to the Controller and
Chief Financial Officer (&#147;CFO&#148;) of Kraft Foods Inc. by the Controller of Altria
Group,&nbsp;Inc. on behalf of Manager, for review and approval. Approval by the
CFO of Kraft Foods Inc. and the CFO of Altria Group,&nbsp;Inc. will constitute
approval by the Manager and Kraft of the estimate of the fixed and variable
expenses for the ensuing year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.5</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Insurance</u>.
Kraft shall pay all costs and expenses relating to the insurance required to be
borne by Kraft pursuant to Article&nbsp;5 and any other applicable provision of
this Agreement.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.6</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Facilities
and Equipment</u>. Kraft shall be responsible, at its sole cost and expense, to
provide (and subsequently repair or replace as necessary) the Hangar Facility
at the Base of </h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Operations and keep the Ground Lease in

Ground Lease.</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.7</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Manual
Compliance</u>. Kraft agrees to abide by and advise its passengers of all
applicable procedures set forth in the Manual.&#160;
Manager shall deliver to a representative designated by Kraft a copy of
the Manual and any updates.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.8</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Training</u>.
Kraft shall provide Manager with reasonable access to and use of the Aircraft
for the purpose of conducting all training and testing that is necessary for
compliance with the FARs and the Manual (including, without limitation,
proficiency checks, line checks, and type training and certification).</h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h1 style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">ARTICLE&nbsp;FOUR</font></b><font style="text-transform:none;"><br>
USE OF FACILITIES&nbsp;&amp; EQUIPMENT</font></h1>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Use
of Facilities and Equipment</u>. Kraft hereby grants Manager usage of the
Hangar Facility as well as all other of Kraft&#146;s facilities and equipment at the
Base of Operations and access to the Airport Leased Premises as Manager
requires to perform its services relating to the Aircraft, the Hangar Facility
and the Airport Leased Premises during the Term in accordance with this
Agreement.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h1 style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">ARTICLE&nbsp;FIVE</font></b><font style="text-transform:none;"><br>
INSURANCE</font></h1>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Manager
Procured Insurance</u>. During the Term until such time as Kraft is no longer
majority owned by Altria Group,&nbsp;Inc., Manager hereby agrees to arrange for
and procure, at Kraft&#146;s expense, insurance coverage of the types, in the
amounts, and including the special provisions set forth below, under separate
aviation insurance policies relating to the Aircraft (&#147;Manager&#146;s Policies&#148;).&#160; The types, amounts and provisions of the
Manager&#146;s Policies may be varied (at Kraft&#146;s expense) to the extent required by
applicable law or regulation.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>All
risk physical damage (hull) insurance, including war, hijacking and allied
perils coverage, with respect to the Aircraft insuring against any loss, theft
or damage to the Aircraft, and extended coverage with respect to any engines or
parts while removed from the Aircraft, in an amount equal to the agreed value
as listed in Exhibit&nbsp;B hereto, with no deductible. Such insurance shall
provide that all losses shall be adjusted with Kraft and be payable to the
beneficial owner of the Aircraft. Such insurance shall also contain a waiver of
subrogation in favor of Manager.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Aircraft
liability insurance, including war, hijacking and allied perils coverage, with
respect to the Aircraft insuring against liability for bodily injury to or
death of persons, including passengers, and damage to or loss of property, in
an amount not less than Two Hundred Fifty Million Dollars ($250,000,000)
combined limit per occurrence (except with respect to war risks, hijacking and
allied perils coverage, which shall be subject to a policy sub-limit in an
amount not less than Fifty Million Dollars ($50,000,000) combined limit per </h3>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8</font></p>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">occurrence and in the annual aggregate for bodily injury to or death
of, and property damage to, third parties).</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Excess/Umbrella
Liability insurance in excess of the Aviation Liability policy limits set forth
above and where applicable in Exhibit&nbsp;B.&#160;
Such Excess/Umbrella policy will include the provision that the primary
Liability policy be scheduled to such program for full policy limits.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Additional
coverages as set forth in Exhibit&nbsp;B hereto.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(e)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>All
liability coverages required by this Article&nbsp;5.1 (except for clause (c)&nbsp;of
such Article) and Exhibit&nbsp;B hereto shall include the following provisions:</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h4 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>such
insurance shall be primary without any right of contribution from any other
insurance available to Manager or Kraft; and</h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h4>

<h4 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>such
insurance shall contain a standard clause as to cross liability or severability
of interests among insured parties providing that the insurance shall operate
in all respects as if a separate policy had been issued covering each party
insured except for limits of liability.</h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h4>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(f)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>All
insurance required by this Article&nbsp;5.1 and Exhibit&nbsp;B hereto shall
include the following provisions:</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h4 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>such
insurance shall cover the operation of the Aircraft;</h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h4>

<h4 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>such
insurance shall name Kraft Foods Inc. and all of its subsidiaries and
affiliates as the Named Insured and shall name Manager, its affiliates,
successors and assigns and their respective officers, directors, members,
managers, employees, agents and representatives (the &#147;Manager Additional
Insureds&#148;) as additional insureds;</h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h4>

<h4 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iii)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
geographic limits of such insurance shall be worldwide, except that in the case
of war, hijacking and allied perils coverage, the coverage territory shall be
subject to such excluded territories as is usual in the aviation insurance
industry;</h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h4>

<h4 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iv)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>such
insurance shall provide that not less than thirty (30) calendar days advance
written notice (except ten (10)&nbsp;days written notice for non-payment of
premium and such shorter period as is customarily available under the war,
hijacking and allied perils insurance) shall be given to Manager and Kraft of
cancellation by any party or adverse material change or reduction in the limits
of coverage applicable to Manager or Kraft under the policies; and</h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h4>

<h4 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(v)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>such
insurance shall contain an invalidation of interest/breach of warranty clause
in favor of Manager Additional Insureds providing that the coverage afforded to
such parties will not be voided or invalidated by any act or neglect of Kraft
or any other insured party.</h4>
