<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(g)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Manager
shall provide to Kraft prior to the first operation of the Aircraft under
Manager&#146;s Policies an insurance certificate reflecting the coverage required by
this Agreement and thereafter, when it becomes available, a copy of the policy
showing the applicable coverages.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.2</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Kraft
Provided Insurance</u>. If at any time during the Term, Kraft is no longer
majority owned by Altria Group,&nbsp;Inc., Kraft shall immediately arrange and
procure, at Kraft&#146;s expense, insurance for the Aircraft (&#147;Kraft&#146;s Policies&#148;).&#160; The provisions of Kraft&#146;s Policies shall be
at least as comprehensive and advantageous as the provisions of Manager&#146;s
Policies, including terms, limitations, conditions and exclusions, and shall
provide the specific coverages and provisions outlined in Articles 5.1(a)-(f)&nbsp;and
5.2(a)&nbsp;and Exhibit&nbsp;B. Furthermore, Kraft&#146;s Policies shall be issued
by an insurance company reasonably acceptable to Manager. Upon Kraft&#146;s notice
to Manager of commencement of insurance coverage under Kraft&#146;s insurance,
Manager&#146;s responsibilities under Article&nbsp;5.1 above shall cease.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Kraft
shall provide to Manager (with its notice of commencement of insurance coverage
as described in this Article&nbsp;5.2) an insurance certificate reflecting the
coverage required by this Agreement and thereafter, when it becomes available,
a copy of the policy showing the applicable coverages. The insurance policy
shall waive all rights of subrogation against the Manager Additional Insureds
and shall recognize in writing this Agreement.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.3</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Manager&#146;s
Insurance Obligations</u>. During the Term, Manager will maintain in full force
and effect, at its own expense:</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Workers&#146;
Compensation Coverage that provides applicable statutory benefits and Employer
Liability Coverage in an amount of not less than Five Hundred Thousand Dollars
($500,000) covering all employees of Manager.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Commercial
General Liability insurance, including premises liability coverage, in the
amount of Five Million Dollars ($5,000,000) per occurrence, and products and
completed operations coverage in the amount of Ten Million Dollars ($10,000,000)
per occurrence and in the aggregate.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Fire
and extended coverage insurance on Manager&#146;s personal property, trade fixtures
and equipment located in or at the Hangar Facility, in an amount equal to the
full replacement value thereof.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.4</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Kraft&#146;s
Insurance Obligations</u>. In addition to and notwithstanding Articles 5.1 and
5.2 above, during the Term, Kraft will maintain in full force and effect, at
its own expense:</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Commercial
General Liability insurance, including premises liability and environmental
coverage,&#160; in the amount of Five Million
Dollars ($5,000,000) per occurrence, and products and completed operations
coverage in the amount of Ten Million Dollars ($10,000,000) combined single
limit per occurrence and in the aggregate.</h3>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Fire
and extended coverage insurance on Kraft&#146;s personal property, trade fixtures
and equipment located in or at the Hangar Facility, in an amount equal to the
full replacement value thereof.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>&#147;All
Risk Property&#148; insurance coverage for the Hangar Facility valued on a &#147;replacement
cost&#148; basis.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.5</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Insurance
Validity</u>. In the event that any insurance on the Aircraft which is required
by this Article&nbsp;5 is invalidated for any reason, the Aircraft shall not be
operated until such time as all such insurance is again valid and in full force
and effect.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h1 style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">ARTICLE&nbsp;SIX</font></b><font style="text-transform:none;"><br>
INDEPENDENT CONTRACTOR</font></h1>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Independent
Contractor</u>. Manager shall be deemed to be an independent contractor.&#160; Manager shall be free to devote to its other
business such portion of its entire time, energy, efforts and skill, as it sees
fit.&#160; Manager shall have no mandatory
duties, except those which are specifically set out in this Agreement.&#160; Nothing contained in this Agreement shall be
regarded as creating any relationship (employer/employee, joint venture,
partnership) between the parties other than as set forth herein.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.2</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>No
Agent Status</u>. Except as specifically set forth in Article&nbsp;2.3, Manager
shall never at any time during the Term become the agent of Kraft and Kraft
shall not be responsible for the acts or omissions of Manager or its agents
except as set forth herein.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.3</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>No
Employee Status</u>. No employee of Manager will, at any time, represent
himself or herself to be an employee of Kraft.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h1 style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">ARTICLE&nbsp;SEVEN</font></b><font style="text-transform:none;"><br>
ALTERATIONS</font></h1>

<h1 style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;">&nbsp;</font></h1>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Alterations</u>.&#160; Manager shall not have the right to alter,
modify or make any additions or improvements to the Aircraft or engines, other
than those necessary to obtain and maintain FAA certification, to maintain the
Aircraft in accordance with the terms hereof or to ensure the Aircraft conforms
to Manager&#146;s criteria and guidelines for aircraft owned and operated by Manager
including alterations to the Aircraft necessary to ensure that the Aircraft are
substantially similar to the aircraft of the same make and model flown by the
flight crew for the Aircraft, without prior written permission from Kraft. All
such alterations, modifications, additions and improvements as are so made
shall become the property of Kraft and shall be subject to the terms of this
Agreement.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h1 style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">ARTICLE&nbsp;EIGHT</font></b><font style="text-transform:none;"><br>
TITLE</font></h1>

<h1 style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;">&nbsp;</font></h1>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Title</u>.&#160; Kraft has the right to operate the Aircraft
pursuant to that certain Dry Lease dated as of December&nbsp;22, 2004 between
Kraft and Kraft Foods Aviation, LLC, the beneficial owner of the Aircraft, and
has full right, power and authority and has secured all necessary consents to
enter into this Agreement with Manager.&#160;
Kraft acquired the Hangar Facility from </h2>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Manager pursuant to the Purchase and Sale
Agreement dated as of December&nbsp;15, 2005 between Manager and Kraft.&#160; Kraft became the lessee under the Ground
Lease pursuant to the Assignment of Lease to Airport Agreement No.&nbsp;HP-695
dated as of December&nbsp;16, 2005, 2005 and executed by Milwaukee County,
Wisconsin, Manager and Kraft.&#160; It is
expressly understood and agreed that this is a management contract, and that
Manager acquires no ownership, title, property rights or interests in or to the
Aircraft and their engines, accessories and equipment or the Hangar Facility or
the Airport Leased Premises.</font></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h1 style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">ARTICLE&nbsp;NINE</font></b><font style="text-transform:none;"><br>
RISK OF LOSS OR DAMAGE TO AIRCRAFT AND/OR THE HANGAR FACILITY</font></h1>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Risk
of Loss or Damage.</u>&#160; Risk of loss or
damage to the Aircraft and/or the Hangar Facility shall be borne by Kraft. If,
during the Term, any of the Aircraft is destroyed, lost or damaged beyond
repair, this Agreement shall terminate immediately, as to such Aircraft, unless
otherwise agreed</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h1 style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">ARTICLE&nbsp;TEN</font></b><font style="text-transform:none;"><br>
INDEMNIFICATION</font></h1>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Indemnification</u>.
Each party to this Agreement hereby indemnifies and holds harmless the other
party and its respective officers, directors, partners, employees, shareholders
and affiliates for any claim, damage, loss or reasonable expense, including
reasonable attorneys&#146; fees, resulting from bodily injury or property damage to
third parties caused by an occurrence and arising out of the ownership,
maintenance or use of the Aircraft which results from the negligence or willful
misconduct of such indemnifying party (an &#147;Indemnified Loss&#148;), provided,
however, that neither party to this Agreement will be liable for any
Indemnified Loss:</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>to
the extent that such loss is covered by the insurance policies described in Article&nbsp;5
(the &#147;Policies&#148;), or in the event the other party fails to maintain the
insurance coverages it is required to maintain pursuant to Article&nbsp;5, such
loss would have been covered under the required coverages had they been in
effect;</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>with
respect to a loss covered by the Policies, to the extent that the amount of
such loss exceeds the policy limits required by Article&nbsp;5;</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>with
respect to a loss consisting of expenses incurred in connection with a loss
covered in whole or in part by the Policies, to the extent that such expenses
are not fully covered by the Policies, or</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>to
the extent of the comparative negligence or willful misconduct of the
indemnified party or its officers, directors, partners, employees, shareholders
and affiliates.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.2</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Indemnification
by Manager</u>. Manager will indemnify Kraft for direct physical damage to the
Aircraft proven to have been caused by Manager&#146;s gross negligence (&#147;Gross
Negligence Aircraft Damage&#148;); provided, however, that Manager will not
indemnify Kraft for any Gross Negligence Aircraft Damage:</h2>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">12</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

</font></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>to
the extent that coverage for such damage is provided by Manager&#146;s Policies
required to be maintained by Manager by Article&nbsp;5 and Exhibit&nbsp;B;</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>with
respect to such damage for which coverage is provided by Manager&#146;s Policies, to
the extent that the amount of such damage exceeds the agreed insured value
specified in Exhibit&nbsp;B;</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>to
the extent that coverage for such damage is provided by Kraft&#146;s Policies
required to be maintained by Kraft by Article&nbsp;5 and Exhibit&nbsp;B, or in
the event Kraft fails to maintain such required insurance coverages, coverage
for such damage would have been provided under such required coverages had they
been in effect; or</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>with
respect to such damage for which coverage is provided by Kraft&#146;s Policies, to
the extent that the amount of such damage exceeds the agreed insured value
specified in Exhibit&nbsp;B.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If any Gross Negligence Aircraft Damage is
not covered by Manager&#146;s or Kraft&#146;s Policies solely because it is less than an
applicable deductible amount set forth in Exhibit&nbsp;B, Manager will
indemnify Kraft for the amount of any such damage up to the amount of such
deductible. Manager will not indemnify Kraft for any other uninsured damage to
the Aircraft.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.3</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>LIMITATION
OF LIABILITY</u>. EACH PARTY ACKNOWLEDGES AND AGREES THAT</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>THE
PROCEEDS OF INSURANCE TO WHICH IT IS ENTITLED;</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>ITS
RIGHTS TO INDEMNIFICATION FROM THE OTHER PARTY UNDER ARTICLE&nbsp;10.1 (AND IN
THE CASE OF KRAFT, ITS RIGHTS TO INDEMNIFICATION UNDER ARTICLE&nbsp;10.2) (AND
IN THE CASE OF MANAGER, ITS RIGHTS TO INDEMNIFICATION UNDER ARTICLES 2.3 AND
10.4); AND</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>ITS
RIGHT TO DIRECT DAMAGES ARISING IN CONTRACT FROM A MATERIAL BREACH OF THE OTHER
PARTY&#146;S OBLIGATIONS UNDER THIS AGREEMENT ARE THE SOLE REMEDIES FOR ANY DAMAGE,
LOSS OR EXPENSE ARISING OUT OF THIS AGREEMENT OR THE SERVICES PROVIDED
HEREUNDER OR CONTEMPLATED HEREBY.&#160; KRAFT
WAIVES ALL RIGHTS OF RECOVERY AGAINST MANAGER AND MANAGER ADDITIONAL INSUREDS
FOR ANY LOSS OR DAMAGE TO THE AIRCRAFT, EXCEPT AS SET FORTH IN ARTICLE&nbsp;10.2
ABOVE.&#160; EXCEPT AS EXPRESSLY SET FORTH IN
THIS ARTICLE&nbsp;10.3 AND ARTICLE&nbsp;10.4, EACH PARTY WAIVES ANY RIGHT TO
RECOVER ANY DAMAGE, LOSS OR EXPENSE ARISING OUT OF THIS AGREEMENT OR THE
SERVICES PROVIDED HEREUNDER OR CONTEMPLATED HEREBY.&#160; IN NO EVENT SHALL EITHER PARTY BE LIABLE FOR
OR HAVE ANY DUTY FOR INDEMNIFICATION OR CONTRIBUTION TO THE OTHER PARTY FOR ANY
CLAIMED INDIRECT, SPECIAL, INCIDENTAL, CONSEQUENTIAL OR PUNITIVE DAMAGES, OR
FOR ANY DAMAGES CONSISTING OF DAMAGES FOR LOSS OF USE, REVENUE, PROFIT,
BUSINESS OPPORTUNITIES AND THE LIKE, OR DEPRECIATION OR DIMINUTION IN VALUE OF
THE AIRCRAFT, EVEN IF THE </h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">PARTY HAD BEEN ADVISED, OR KNEW OR SHOULD HAVE KNOWN OF THE POSSIBILITY

apply to the extent that Kraft&#146;s Policies have failed to provide the insurance
coverage required by Article&nbsp;5, including Exhibit&nbsp;B. Furthermore,
Kraft agrees to indemnify Manager for any Indemnified Loss resulting from the
failure of Kraft&#146;s Policies to comply with the requirements of Article&nbsp;5,
including Exhibit&nbsp;B.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.5</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Survival</u>.
The provisions of this Article&nbsp;10 will survive the termination or
expiration of this Agreement.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h1 style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">ARTICLE&nbsp;ELEVEN</font></b><font style="text-transform:none;"><br>
MISCELLANEOUS PROVISIONS</font></h1>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Base
of Operations, Hangar Facility, Ground Lease and Airport Leased Premises</u></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For purposes of this Agreement:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
Base of Operations of the Aircraft shall be General Mitchell International
Airport (MKE), Milwaukee, Wisconsin;</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
Hangar Facility shall consist of the hangar, fuel farm, fuel truck (when
transferred by Manager to Kraft), aircraft ramp facilities, parking facilities,
office space and aircraft support equipment and spare parts owned by Kraft
which are located on the Airport Leased Premises;</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
Ground Lease shall mean that certain Lease Agreement No.&nbsp;HP-695 dated as
of July&nbsp;14, 1980, as amended, with respect to the Airport Leased Premises;
and</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
Airport Leased Premises shall mean those premises at the Base of Operations
which are the subject of the Ground Lease and on which the Hangar Facility is
located.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.2</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Entire
Agreement</u>. This Agreement constitutes the entire understanding between the
parties as of the Effective Date and supersedes all prior agreements between
the parties with respect to the subject matter hereof.&#160; Any change, modification or amendment to this
Agreement must be in writing signed by both parties.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.6</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Invalidity</u>.
In the event that any one or more of the provisions of this Agreement shall be
determined to be invalid, unenforceable or illegal, such invalidity,
unenforceability and illegality shall not affect any other provisions of this
Agreement, and the Agreement shall be construed as if such invalid,
unenforceable or illegal provisions had never been contained herein.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.7</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Force
Majeure</u>. Exclusive of Kraft&#146;s obligations to pay for the operating expenses
and other expenses associated with the Aircraft, each party shall be relieved
of its obligations hereunder in the event and to the extent that the party&#146;s
performance is delayed or prevented by any cause reasonably beyond such party&#146;s

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.8</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Waiver</u>.

hereunder by either party shall be construed as a waiver of such right or

undertakings, obligations and agreements contained herein shall be cumulative
and not mutually exclusive.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.9</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Assignment</u>.
Neither this Agreement nor any party&#146;s interest herein shall be assignable to
any other party without the consent of the other party. This Agreement shall
inure to the benefit of and be binding upon the parties hereto, their heirs,
representatives and successors.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.10</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Confidentiality</u>.
Manager and Kraft shall not disclose to any third party (other than their
respective affiliates) in any manner information regarding the terms of this
Agreement without the non-disclosing party&#146;s prior written consent; provided,
however, that neither party shall be prohibited from making any disclosures to
the extent required by law.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.11</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Review
of Records</u>. Each party shall permit the other, upon reasonable request, to
review its accounting and other cost records relating to the Aircraft, so the
other party can conduct an audit of such records as that other party reasonably
deems necessary.</h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h1 style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">ARTICLE&nbsp;TWELVE</font></b><font style="text-transform:none;"><br>
APPLICABLE LAW</font></h1>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;text-justify:inter-ideograph;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">12.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Governing
Law and Jurisdiction</u>. This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in
accordance with the laws of the State of New York.&#160; Without limiting in any way the jurisdiction
of the courts of any state, nation or province, or Manager&#146;s right to invoke
the jurisdiction of such courts, Kraft hereby consents to the jurisdiction of
the courts of the United States of America and the State of New York in any
dispute which arises out of this Agreement and agrees that service of process
shall be sufficient if made on the Secretary of State of New York with a copy
to be sent, by registered mail, to Kraft at the address set forth in Article&nbsp;11.3
above.</h2>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">16</font></p>

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

this Agreement as of the day and year first above written.</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit&nbsp;10.3</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h1 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;text-decoration:underline;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">ENVIRONMENTAL AGREEMENT</font></u></h1>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This Environmental Agreement is made this 16th day of December, 2005,
by and between <b><font style="font-weight:bold;">ALTRIA CORPORATE SERVICES,
INC. (f/k/a PHILIP MORRIS MANAGEMENT CORP.)</font></b>, a New York corporation
(&#147;Altria&#148;) and <b><font style="font-weight:bold;">KRAFT FOODS GLOBAL, INC.</font></b></font>(&#147;Kraft&#148;),
a Delaware corporation.</p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">W I T N E S S
E T H</font></h2>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">WHEREAS, Altria and Milwaukee County, Wisconsin, are parties to that
certain Lease Agreement, dated July&nbsp;14, 1980, Airport Agreement No.&nbsp;HP-695,
as amended by Amendment No.&nbsp;1 to Airport Lease Agreement No.&nbsp;HP-695
as of December&nbsp;31, 1995 and Amendment No.&nbsp;2 to Airport Lease
Agreement No.&nbsp;HP-695 as of December&nbsp;16, 2005 (the &#147;Original Lease&#148;)
with respect to certain property (the &#147;Property&#148;) located at General Mitchell
International Airport (&#147;Airport&#148;); and</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">WHEREAS, Altria and Kraft are parties to the certain Purchase and Sale
Agreement (&#147;PSA&#148;) dated December&nbsp;15, 2005, by which Altria agreed to sell
and transfer to Kraft, and Kraft agreed to purchase and accept from Altria, all
of Altria&#146;s rights, title and interests in the Original Lease and certain other
property described in the PSA on the terms and conditions set forth therein;
and</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">WHEREAS, Altria, Kraft, and Milwaukee County, Wisconsin, are parties to
that certain Assignment of Lease dated December&nbsp;16, 2005, (&#147;Date of
Assignment&#148;) by which Altria assigned and transferred all right, title, and
interest of Altria in and to the Original Lease to Kraft and by which Kraft
accepted such assignment and agreed to perform, observe, and accept all such
obligations, covenants and conditions contained in the Original Lease on the
part of Altria from and after the Date of Assignment; and</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">WHEREAS, Altria and Kraft are parties to that certain Management
Agreement dated December&nbsp;16, 2005 (the &#147;Management Agreement&#148;) by which
Altria has agreed to maintain and operate the Property for the purposes for
which it is intended on the terms and conditions set forth therein; and</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">WHEREAS, Altria and Kraft seek to define and allocate responsibility
for certain environmental matters pertaining to the Property as set forth in
this Agreement even though other representations, warranties, rights and
obligations contained in the PSA will not survive after the effective date of
the PSA or will expire within a fixed period of time thereafter; and</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">WHEREAS, Altria and Tennessee Gas Pipeline Company, a Delaware
corporation (successor by name change to Tenneco Inc.) (&#147;Tenneco&#148;), which
occupied the Property before Altria, are parties to that certain Agreement,
dated December&nbsp;29, 1995, as amended by Letter Agreement No.&nbsp;1 as of December&nbsp;29,
1995 and Letter Agreement No.&nbsp;2 Airport Lease Agreement as of December&nbsp;31,
1995 (collectively the &#147;Tenneco Agreement&#148;); and</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">WHEREAS, Altria and Kraft seek to define and set forth the assignment
of certain rights and obligations under the Tenneco Agreement from Altria to
Kraft.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\mgovind\05-21974-1\task711885\21974-1-ke.htm',USER='mgovindarajulu',CD='Dec 18 11:40 2005' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the foregoing premises and of the
mutual covenants, representations and warranties herein set forth, the parties
hereto hereby covenant and agree as follows:</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Environmental
Responsibility</u>.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Altria
shall be responsible for all conditions, releases or discharges on the Property
involving any hazardous or toxic substances, materials, or wastes including,
without limitation, petroleum, as these terms are used or defined in applicable
local, state or federal environmental laws and regulations (collectively &#147;hazardous
or toxic materials&#148;) (1)&nbsp;first occurring from September&nbsp;1, 1993, to December&nbsp;16,
2005, (2)&nbsp;relating to or originating from conditions that first existed
from September&nbsp;1, 1993, to December&nbsp;16, 2005, or (3)&nbsp;relating to
such further cleanup of UST #5 as may be required, if at all, under the
Original Lease or the Assignment of Lease dated December&nbsp;16, 2005.&#160; Except as provided for in Paragraph 1.B.
below, Kraft shall be responsible for other conditions, releases or discharges
involving any hazardous or toxic materials on the Property as may first occur
on and after December&nbsp;16, 2005.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">B.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Altria
shall also be responsible for all conditions, releases or discharges on the
Property involving any hazardous or toxic materials caused by the willful
misconduct of Altria and its employees during the term of the Management
Agreement, except to the extent such acts are directed by Kraft, its employees,
or contractors.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">C.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Kraft will maintain in
full force and effect, at its own expense, any financial instruments necessary to comply with the requirements of
subpart H of 40 CFR part 280 and the corresponding applicable state regulations
including, without limitation, Wisconsin Admin Code ch. Comm 10, subchapter
VIII, regarding Kraft&#146;s financial responsibility for taking corrective action
and for compensating third parties for bodily injury and property damage caused
by accidental releases from the operation of petroleum underground storage
tanks.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Indemnification
as to Environmental Matters</u>.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Altria
shall indemnify and hold harmless Kraft from and against any and all claims,
demands, damages, losses, costs and expenses, including without limitation,
court costs and reasonable attorney&#146;s fees, arising from (1)&nbsp;any
violations by Altria of laws, orders, rules, regulations, requirements,
guidelines or demands of any local, state or federal governmental agency or
other authority based upon applicable environmental laws relating to the
Property and occurring on or before the date hereof, and (2)&nbsp;all
conditions, releases or discharges involving any hazardous or toxic materials
on the Property (a)&nbsp;first occurring from September&nbsp;1, 1993, to December&nbsp;16,
2005, relating to or originating from conditions that first existed from September&nbsp;1,
1993, to December&nbsp;16, 2005, or relating to such further cleanup of UST #5
as may be required, if at all, under the Original Lease or the Assignment of
Lease dated December&nbsp;16, 2005, or (b)&nbsp;caused by the willful
misconduct of Altria, its employees and contractors, during the term of the
Management Agreement, except to the extent such acts are directed by Kraft, its
employees, or contractors.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">B.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Kraft
shall indemnify and hold harmless Altria from and against any and all claims,
demands, damages, losses, costs and expenses, including without limitation,
court </p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\mgovind\05-21974-1\task711885\21974-1-ke.htm',USER='mgovindarajulu',CD='Dec 18 11:40 2005' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">costs
and reasonable attorney&#146;s fees, arising from (1)&nbsp;any violations by Kraft
of laws, orders, rules, regulations, requirements, guidelines or demands of any
local, state of federal governmental agency or other authority based upon
applicable environmental laws relating to the Property and occurring on or
after the date hereof, and (2)&nbsp;all conditions, releases or discharges
involving any hazardous or toxic materials on the Property first occurring on
or after December&nbsp;16, 2005, except to the extent caused by the willful
misconduct of Altria and its employees during the term of the Management
Agreement (unless such acts are directed by Kraft, its employees, or
contractors).</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Defense
of Action</u>.&#160; In the case of any action
or proceeding brought against Altria or Kraft, as the case may be, by reason of
any such claim indemnified against pursuant to this Agreement, upon notice, the
other party shall defend the action or proceeding by counsel reasonably
acceptable to the other.&#160; This
requirement is conditioned upon receipt by the indemnifying party of timely
written notice of, and the opportunity to defend, any such claims and upon the
cooperation of the party against whom the claim is made in the defense of such
claim.&#160; Timely written notice for
purposes of this Paragraph means written notice within fourteen (14) days of
receipt of any written claim, demand, legal process or paper relating to such
claim provided, however, that, in an action to enforce the indemnity, late
notice will not be a defense absent a showing of prejudice to the indemnitor.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Assignment
of Rights Against Tenneco</u>.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Altria
hereby assigns and transfers to Kraft all the rights and interests of Altria in
and to the Tenneco Agreement.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">B.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Kraft
hereby accepts said assignment and agrees to perform, observe, and accept all
the obligations, covenants and conditions on Altria contained therein to be
performed and observed from and after the date hereon.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Responsibility
for Site Work</u>.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Stormwater
Discharge.&#160; Altria shall take such action
as may be required to obtain a general WPDES permit for the lawful discharge of
water from the sump pump associated with the fuel farm along East College
Avenue to the storm sewer.&#160; This
obligation shall terminate upon receipt of the applicable permit.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">B.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>UST
#5.&#160; Altria shall take such action as may
be required to achieve closure of the WDNR file on UST #5, including but not
limited to assuring that (1)&nbsp;necessary well abandonment forms are filed
with WDNR and (2)&nbsp;an adequate deed restriction is recorded (with proof of
recording filed with WDNR).&#160; This
obligation shall terminate upon confirmation that WDNR has closed its file on
this matter.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Entire
Agreement; Headings; Counterparts</u>.&#160;
This Agreement constitutes the entire agreement and understanding of the
parties hereto with respect to the subject matter hereof and supersedes all
prior negotiations and understandings, whether written or oral, of the parties
hereto with respect to the subject matter hereof, including, but not limited
to, any language in or interpretation of the PSA contrary to the terms of this
Agreement.&#160; The headings in this
Agreement are for the purposes of reference only and shall not limit or
otherwise affect the </p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">meaning
hereof.&#160; This Agreement may be executed
and delivered by the parties hereto in one or more counterparts, each of which
shall be an original but all of which together shall constitute one instrument.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Binding
Affect</u>.&#160; This Agreement is binding
upon and inures to the benefit of the parties hereto and their respective
successors and assigns.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Applicable
Law</u>.&#160; This agreement shall be
governed and construed in accordance with the laws of the State of Wisconsin.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Facsimile
Signatures</u>.&#160; Altria and Kraft agree
that signatures on documents delivered by facsimile transmission shall be
binding on all parties, and respectively agree to provide an originally signed
copy of any document delivered by facsimile within five (5)&nbsp;days after
such delivery.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Counterparts</u>.&#160; This agreement may be executed in
counterparts, each of which shall be deemed an original, but all of which
together shall constitute one and the same instrument.</p>
